info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Family
info:15 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted July 14, 2021
msg:1. The day before check-in, I asked for information on the phone. During the epidemic, I did a good job and asked about my room preferences. Later, it proved that the high floors and the view were satisfied.
2. Check in at 5:30 in the afternoon, and the front desk gave Hilton cookies, which the children liked. There are welcome fruits. The room faces the sea and you can look at Gulangyu Island. The scenery is great!
3. The cleaning was normal on the first day, but it was a bit unexpected on the second day. The floor was not clean and the toiletries were not filled. Called to the front desk, the customer service was very responsible first to arrange the delivery of toiletries, and then called to apologize, and offered a free drink coupon, which is worthy of praise. But we finally forgot to get the drink coupons, haha.
4. Because with two children, the room rate includes two breakfasts. The breakfast cost for two children is a bit high. In consultation with the deputy manager of the breakfast room, he decisively presented a three-day single adult breakfast. Very pleasantly surprised and happy!
5. After checking out, I asked the child for two cookies, and the front desk service was in place.

Great stay experience, cost-effective! highly recommended!
